=== FILE: README.md ===


  # Splash Screen Design

  This is a code bundle for Splash Screen Design. The original project is available at https://www.figma.com/design/ioXJ4m7KAV1pVTiH9PyINn/Splash-Screen-Design.

  ## Running the code

  Run `npm i` to install the dependencies.

  Run `npm run dev` to start the development server.

    </head>

    <body>
      <div id="root"></div>
      <script type="module" src="/src/main.tsx"></script>
    </body>
  </html>

=== FILE: src/App.tsx ===

import { useState } from 'react';
import { SplashScreen } from './components/SplashScreen';
import { OnboardingFlow } from './components/OnboardingFlow';
import { SignInScreen } from './components/SignInScreen';
import { HomeScreen } from './components/HomeScreen';
import { ServiceSelectionScreen } from './components/ServiceSelectionScreen';
import { SelectCarScreen } from './components/SelectCarScreen';
import { AddCarScreen } from './components/AddCarScreen';
import { BookingDateTimeScreen } from './components/BookingDateTimeScreen';
import { ChooseDetailerScreen } from './components/ChooseDetailerScreen';
import { OrderSummaryScreen } from './components/OrderSummaryScreen';
import { PaymentMethodScreen } from './components/PaymentMethodScreen';
import { AddPaymentCardScreen } from './components/AddPaymentCardScreen';
import { LiveTrackingScreen } from './components/LiveTrackingScreen';
import { ServiceProgressScreen } from './components/ServiceProgressScreen';
import { ReceiptRatingScreen } from './components/ReceiptRatingScreen';
import { ProfileScreen } from './components/ProfileScreen';
import { EditProfileScreen } from './components/EditProfileScreen';
import { NotificationsScreen } from './components/NotificationsScreen';
import { HelpSupportScreen } from './components/HelpSupportScreen';
import { OrdersHistoryScreen } from './components/OrdersHistoryScreen';
import { OrderDetailsScreen } from './components/OrderDetailsScreen';

type Screen = 
  | 'splash' 
  | 'onboarding' 
  | 'signin' 
  | 'home' 
  | 'service-selection'
  | 'booking-datetime'
  | 'choose-detailer'
  | 'order-summary'
  | 'select-car' 
  | 'add-car'
  | 'payment-method'
  | 'add-payment-card'
  | 'live-tracking'
  | 'service-progress'
  | 'receipt-rating'
  | 'profile'
  | 'edit-profile'
  | 'notifications'
  | 'help-support'
  | 'orders-history'
  | 'order-details';

type NavigationContext = 'booking' | 'profile' | 'orders';

export default function App() {
  const [currentScreen, setCurrentScreen] = useState<Screen>('splash');
  const [navigationContext, setNavigationContext] = useState<NavigationContext>('booking');

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[#050B12]">
      {/* Mobile Container - 9:16 aspect ratio simulation */}
      <div className="max-w-md mx-auto h-screen relative overflow-hidden bg-[#050B12]">
        {currentScreen === 'splash' && (
          <SplashScreen onComplete={() => setCurrentScreen('onboarding')} />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'onboarding' && (
          <OnboardingFlow onComplete={() => setCurrentScreen('signin')} />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'signin' && (
          <SignInScreen onSignIn={() => setCurrentScreen('home')} />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'home' && (
          <HomeScreen 
            onBookService={() => {
              setNavigationContext('booking');
              setCurrentScreen('service-selection');
            }}
            onSelectCar={() => {
              setNavigationContext('profile');
              setCurrentScreen('select-car');
            }}
            onProfile={() => setCurrentScreen('profile')}
            onOrders={() => {
              setNavigationContext('orders');
              setCurrentScreen('orders-history');
            }}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'service-selection' && (
          <ServiceSelectionScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('home')}
            onContinue={() => setCurrentScreen('booking-datetime')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'booking-datetime' && (
          <BookingDateTimeScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('service-selection')}
            onContinue={() => setCurrentScreen('choose-detailer')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'choose-detailer' && (
          <ChooseDetailerScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('booking-datetime')}
            onContinue={() => setCurrentScreen('order-summary')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'order-summary' && (
          <OrderSummaryScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('choose-detailer')}
            onContinue={() => setCurrentScreen('payment-method')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'select-car' && (
          <SelectCarScreen
            onBack={() => {
              if (navigationContext === 'profile') {
                setCurrentScreen('profile');
              } else {
                setCurrentScreen('order-summary');
              }
            }}
            onAddCar={() => setCurrentScreen('add-car')}
            onContinue={() => {
              if (navigationContext === 'profile') {
                setCurrentScreen('home');
              } else {
                setCurrentScreen('order-summary');
              }
            }}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'add-car' && (
          <AddCarScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('select-car')}
            onSave={() => setCurrentScreen('select-car')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'payment-method' && (
          <PaymentMethodScreen
            onBack={() => {
              if (navigationContext === 'profile') {
                setCurrentScreen('profile');
              } else {
                setCurrentScreen('order-summary');
              }
            }}
            onContinue={() => {
              if (navigationContext === 'profile') {
                setCurrentScreen('home');
              } else {
                setCurrentScreen('live-tracking');
              }
            }}
            onAddCard={() => setCurrentScreen('add-payment-card')}
            showPriceSummary={navigationContext !== 'profile'}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'add-payment-card' && (
          <AddPaymentCardScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('payment-method')}
            onSave={() => setCurrentScreen('payment-method')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'live-tracking' && (
          <LiveTrackingScreen
            onComplete={() => setCurrentScreen('service-progress')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'service-progress' && (
          <ServiceProgressScreen
            onComplete={() => setCurrentScreen('receipt-rating')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'receipt-rating' && (
          <ReceiptRatingScreen
            onComplete={() => setCurrentScreen('home')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'profile' && (
          <ProfileScreen
            onEditProfile={() => setCurrentScreen('edit-profile')}
            onOrders={() => {
              setNavigationContext('orders');
              setCurrentScreen('orders-history');
            }}
            onManageCars={() => {
              setNavigationContext('profile');
              setCurrentScreen('select-car');
            }}
            onPayment={() => {
              setNavigationContext('profile');
              setCurrentScreen('payment-method');
            }}
            onNotifications={() => setCurrentScreen('notifications')}
            onSupport={() => setCurrentScreen('help-support')}
            onSettings={() => setCurrentScreen('edit-profile')}
            onLogout={() => setCurrentScreen('signin')}
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('home')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'edit-profile' && (
          <EditProfileScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('profile')}
            onSave={() => setCurrentScreen('profile')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'notifications' && (
          <NotificationsScreen onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('profile')} />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'help-support' && (
          <HelpSupportScreen onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('profile')} />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'orders-history' && (
          <OrdersHistoryScreen
            onBack={() => {
              if (navigationContext === 'orders') {
                setCurrentScreen('home');
              } else {
                setCurrentScreen('profile');
              }
            }}
            onOrderDetails={(orderId) => setCurrentScreen('order-details')}
          />
        )}

        {currentScreen === 'order-details' && (
          <OrderDetailsScreen
            onBack={() => setCurrentScreen('orders-history')}
            onBookAgain={() => setCurrentScreen('service-selection')}
          />
        )}

        {/* Screen Indicator - for development */}
        <div className="fixed top-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 px-4 py-2 bg-black/50 backdrop-blur-sm rounded-full z-50">
          <p className="text-[#6FF0C4] text-xs font-mono">
            {currentScreen}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

=== FILE: src/components/AddCarScreen.tsx ===

import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronLeft, Upload } from 'lucide-react';

interface AddCarScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
  onSave: () => void;
}

export function AddCarScreen({ onBack, onSave }: AddCarScreenProps) {
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    make: '',
    model: '',
    year: '',
    trim: '',
    license: '',
    color: '',
  });

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    onSave();
  };

  const updateField = (field: string, value: string) => {
    setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }));
  };

  const isFormValid = formData.make && formData.model && formData.year && formData.license;

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-6 flex items-center gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Add a Car
        </h1>
      </div>

      {/* Form - Scrollable */}
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-32">
        {/* Optional Photo Upload */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <button
            type="button"
            className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-3xl p-8 border border-dashed border-[#C6CFD9]/20 transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] hover:border-[#6FF0C4]/30"
          >
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-[#1DA4F3]/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                <Upload className="w-8 h-8 text-[#1DA4F3]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
              </div>
              <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>
                Add Photo (Optional)
              </p>
            </div>
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Form Fields */}
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {/* Make */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Make
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="e.g., BMW"
              value={formData.make}
              onChange={(e) => updateField('make', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>

          {/* Model */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Model
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="e.g., M4"
              value={formData.model}
              onChange={(e) => updateField('model', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>

          {/* Year */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Year
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="e.g., 2022"
              value={formData.year}
              onChange={(e) => updateField('year', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>

          {/* Trim */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Trim <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]/50">(Optional)</span>
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="e.g., Competition Package"
              value={formData.trim}
              onChange={(e) => updateField('trim', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>

          {/* License Plate */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              License Plate
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="e.g., ABC-123"
              value={formData.license}
              onChange={(e) => updateField('license', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>

          {/* Color */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Color <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]/50">(Optional)</span>
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="e.g., Black Sapphire Metallic"
              value={formData.color}
              onChange={(e) => updateField('color', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>

      {/* Bottom CTA */}
      <div className="px-6 pb-8 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#050B12] via-[#050B12] to-transparent pt-6">
        <button
          type="submit"
          onClick={handleSubmit}
          disabled={!isFormValid}
          className={`w-full py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 ${
            isFormValid
              ? 'bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20'
              : 'bg-[#0A1A2F] text-[#C6CFD9]/50 cursor-not-allowed'
          }`}
          style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600 }}
        >
          Save Car
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


=== FILE: src/components/AddPaymentCardScreen.tsx ===

import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronLeft, CreditCard } from 'lucide-react';

interface AddPaymentCardScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
  onSave: () => void;
}

export function AddPaymentCardScreen({ onBack, onSave }: AddPaymentCardScreenProps) {
  const [cardNumber, setCardNumber] = useState('');
  const [expiry, setExpiry] = useState('');
  const [cvc, setCvc] = useState('');
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [setAsDefault, setSetAsDefault] = useState(true);

  const formatCardNumber = (value: string) => {
    const v = value.replace(/\s+/g, '').replace(/[^0-9]/gi, '');
    const matches = v.match(/\d{4,16}/g);
    const match = (matches && matches[0]) || '';
    const parts = [];

    for (let i = 0, len = match.length; i < len; i += 4) {
      parts.push(match.substring(i, i + 4));
    }

    if (parts.length) {
      return parts.join(' ');
    } else {
      return value;
    }
  };

  const formatExpiry = (value: string) => {
    const v = value.replace(/\s+/g, '').replace(/[^0-9]/gi, '');
    if (v.length >= 2) {
      return v.slice(0, 2) + ' / ' + v.slice(2, 4);
    }
    return v;
  };

  const handleCardNumberChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setCardNumber(formatCardNumber(e.target.value));
  };

  const handleExpiryChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setExpiry(formatExpiry(e.target.value));
  };

  const isFormValid = cardNumber.length >= 15 && expiry.length >= 5 && cvc.length >= 3 && name.length > 0;

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-6 flex items-center gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Add Card
        </h1>
      </div>

      {/* Form - Scrollable */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-32">
        {/* Security Statement */}
        <p className="text-[#C6CFD9] text-center mb-8" style={{ fontSize: '0.8125rem' }}>
          Your payment information is encrypted and securely stored.
        </p>

        {/* Minimal Card Visual */}
        <div className="mb-8 bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-3xl p-6 border border-[#C6CFD9]/20">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
            <CreditCard className="w-8 h-8 text-[#C6CFD9]" strokeWidth={1} />
            <div className="w-10 h-6 bg-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded" />
          </div>
          <div className="h-px bg-[#C6CFD9]/10 mb-4" />
          <p className="text-[#C6CFD9] tracking-wider" style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
            {cardNumber || '•••• •••• •••• ••••'}
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Form Fields */}
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {/* Card Number */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Card Number
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="1234 5678 9012 3456"
              value={cardNumber}
              onChange={handleCardNumberChange}
              maxLength={19}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all tracking-wider"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>

          {/* Expiry & CVC Row */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                Expiry Date
              </label>
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="MM / YY"
                value={expiry}
                onChange={handleExpiryChange}
                maxLength={7}
                className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
                style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
              />
            </div>

            <div>
              <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                CVC
              </label>
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="123"
                value={cvc}
                onChange={(e) => setCvc(e.target.value.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').slice(0, 4))}
                maxLength={4}
                className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
                style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Name on Card */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2 px-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Name on Card
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="JOHN DOE"
              value={name}
              onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value.toUpperCase())}
              className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-5 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9]/50 focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem' }}
            />
          </div>

          {/* Default Card Toggle */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between py-4">
            <span className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Set as default payment method
            </span>
            <button
              onClick={() => setSetAsDefault(!setAsDefault)}
              className={`relative w-12 h-7 rounded-full transition-colors duration-200 ${
                setAsDefault ? 'bg-[#6FF0C4]' : 'bg-[#C6CFD9]/30'
              }`}
            >
              <div
                className={`absolute top-1 w-5 h-5 bg-white rounded-full transition-transform duration-200 ${
                  setAsDefault ? 'translate-x-6' : 'translate-x-1'
                }`}
              />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Bottom CTA */}
      <div className="px-6 pb-8 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#050B12] via-[#050B12] to-transparent pt-6">
        <button
          onClick={onSave}
          disabled={!isFormValid}
          className={`w-full py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 ${
            isFormValid
              ? 'bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20'
              : 'bg-[#0A1A2F] text-[#C6CFD9]/50 cursor-not-allowed'
          }`}
          style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600 }}
        >
          Save Card
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronLeft, Calendar, Clock } from 'lucide-react';

interface BookingDateTimeScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
  onContinue: () => void;
}

const dates = [
  { day: 'Mon', date: 13 },
  { day: 'Tue', date: 14 },
  { day: 'Wed', date: 15 },
  { day: 'Thu', date: 16, available: true },
  { day: 'Fri', date: 17, available: true },
  { day: 'Sat', date: 18, available: true },
  { day: 'Sun', date: 19, available: true },
];

const timeSlots = [
  { time: '8:00 AM', available: true },
  { time: '9:30 AM', available: true },
  { time: '11:00 AM', available: true },
  { time: '1:00 PM', available: true },
  { time: '3:30 PM', available: true },
  { time: '5:00 PM', available: false },
  { time: '6:30 PM', available: false },
  { time: '8:00 PM', available: false },
];

export function BookingDateTimeScreen({ onBack, onContinue }: BookingDateTimeScreenProps) {
  const [selectedDate, setSelectedDate] = useState<number>(16);
  const [selectedTime, setSelectedTime] = useState<string>('');

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-6 flex items-center gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors active:scale-95"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Choose Date & Time
        </h1>
      </div>

      {/* Scrollable Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-32">
        {/* Date Picker */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-5">
            <Calendar className="w-5 h-5 text-[#6FF0C4]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
            <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
              Select Date
            </h3>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3 overflow-x-auto pb-2 scrollbar-hide">
            {dates.map((date) => {
              const isSelected = selectedDate === date.date;
              const isAvailable = date.available;

              return (
                <button
                  key={date.date}
                  onClick={() => isAvailable && setSelectedDate(date.date)}
                  disabled={!isAvailable}
                  className={`flex-shrink-0 w-20 py-4 rounded-2xl transition-all duration-200 ${
                    isSelected
                      ? 'bg-[#0A1A2F] border-2 border-[#6FF0C4] shadow-lg shadow-[#6FF0C4]/20'
                      : isAvailable
                      ? 'bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-white/5 active:scale-95 hover:border-white/10'
                      : 'bg-[#0A1A2F]/30 border border-white/5 opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed'
                  }`}
                >
                  <p
                    className={`mb-1 ${
                      isSelected ? 'text-[#6FF0C4]' : 'text-[#C6CFD9]'
                    }`}
                    style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}
                  >
                    {date.day}
                  </p>
                  <p
                    className={`${isSelected ? 'text-[#F5F7FA]' : 'text-[#F5F7FA]'}`}
                    style={{ fontSize: '1.5rem', fontWeight: 600 }}
                  >
                    {date.date}
                  </p>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Time Slot Grid */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-5">
            <Clock className="w-5 h-5 text-[#1DA4F3]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
            <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
              Select Time
            </h3>
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            {timeSlots.map((slot) => {
              const isSelected = selectedTime === slot.time;
              const isAvailable = slot.available;

              return (
                <button
                  key={slot.time}
                  onClick={() => isAvailable && setSelectedTime(slot.time)}
                  disabled={!isAvailable}
                  className={`py-4 rounded-2xl transition-all duration-200 ${
                    isSelected
                      ? 'bg-[#0A1A2F] border-2 border-[#6FF0C4] shadow-lg shadow-[#6FF0C4]/20'
                      : isAvailable
                      ? 'bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-white/5 active:scale-95 hover:border-white/10'
                      : 'bg-[#0A1A2F]/30 border border-white/5 opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed'
                  }`}
                  style={{ minHeight: '56px' }}
                >
                  <p
                    className={`${
                      isSelected ? 'text-[#6FF0C4]' : isAvailable ? 'text-[#F5F7FA]' : 'text-[#C6CFD9]'
                    }`}
                    style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}
                  >
                    {slot.time}
                  </p>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Bottom CTA */}
      <div className="px-6 pb-8 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#050B12] via-[#050B12] to-transparent pt-6">
        <button
          onClick={onContinue}
          disabled={!selectedTime}
          className={`w-full py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 ${
            selectedTime
              ? 'bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20'
              : 'bg-[#0A1A2F] text-[#C6CFD9]/50 cursor-not-allowed'
          }`}
          style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600, minHeight: '56px' }}
        >
          Continue
        </button>
      </div>

      <style>{`
        .scrollbar-hide::-webkit-scrollbar {
          display: none;
        }
        .scrollbar-hide {
          -ms-overflow-style: none;
          scrollbar-width: none;
        }
      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
}

                      className={`w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9] flex-shrink-0 transition-transform duration-200 ${
                        isExpanded ? 'rotate-90' : ''
                      }`}
                      strokeWidth={1.5}
                    />
                  </div>
                  {isExpanded && (
                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9] mt-3" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>
                      {faq.answer}
                    </p>
                  )}
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Contact Us */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-4" style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
            Contact Us
          </h3>
          <div className="bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl border border-white/5 overflow-hidden">
            {contactOptions.map((option, index) => {
              const Icon = option.icon;
              const isLast = index === contactOptions.length - 1;
              return (
                <button
                  key={index}
                  className={`w-full flex items-center gap-4 px-5 py-4 transition-all duration-200 active:bg-[#050B12] ${
                    !isLast ? 'border-b border-[#C6CFD9]/10' : ''
                  }`}
                >
                  <Icon className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                  <div className="flex-1 text-left">
                    <p className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-0.5" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                      {option.label}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.8125rem' }}>
                      {option.subtitle}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Policies */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-4" style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
            Policies
          </h3>
          <div className="bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl border border-white/5 overflow-hidden">
            {policies.map((policy, index) => {
              const isLast = index === policies.length - 1;
              return (
                <button
                  key={index}
                  className={`w-full flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 transition-all duration-200 active:bg-[#050B12] ${
                    !isLast ? 'border-b border-[#C6CFD9]/10' : ''
                  }`}
                >
                  <span className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                    {policy.label}
                  </span>
                  <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

=== FILE: src/components/NotificationsScreen.tsx ===

import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronLeft } from 'lucide-react';

interface NotificationsScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
}

interface ToggleSetting {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  description: string;
  enabled: boolean;
  locked?: boolean;
}

export function NotificationsScreen({ onBack }: NotificationsScreenProps) {
  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<ToggleSetting[]>([
    { id: 'push', label: 'Push Notifications', description: 'Receive updates about your bookings', enabled: true },
    { id: 'sms', label: 'SMS Notifications', description: 'Get text messages for important updates', enabled: true },
    { id: 'email', label: 'Email Notifications', description: 'Receive booking confirmations via email', enabled: false },
  ]);

  const [serviceUpdates, setServiceUpdates] = useState<ToggleSetting[]>([
    { id: 'booking', label: 'Booking Confirmations', description: 'Confirmation when you book a service', enabled: true },
    { id: 'ontheway', label: 'Detailer On The Way', description: 'When your detailer is approaching', enabled: true },
    { id: 'arrival', label: 'Arrival Alerts', description: 'When your detailer has arrived', enabled: true },
    { id: 'status', label: 'Cleaning Status Updates', description: 'Progress updates during service', enabled: true },
    { id: 'complete', label: 'Completion Notifications', description: 'When your service is complete', enabled: true },
  ]);

  const [reminders, setReminders] = useState<ToggleSetting[]>([
    { id: 'upcoming', label: 'Upcoming Appointment Reminders', description: 'Notifies you 30 minutes before', enabled: true },
    { id: 'maintenance', label: 'Maintenance Suggestions', description: 'Helpful car care tips', enabled: false },
  ]);

  const [promotional, setPromotional] = useState<ToggleSetting[]>([
    { id: 'offers', label: 'Special Offers', description: 'Exclusive deals and promotions', enabled: false },
    { id: 'discounts', label: 'Discount Announcements', description: 'Seasonal savings alerts', enabled: false },
  ]);

  const [system, setSystem] = useState<ToggleSetting[]>([
    { id: 'security', label: 'Account Security Alerts', description: 'You will always receive security notifications', enabled: true, locked: true },
    { id: 'payment', label: 'Payment Status Notifications', description: 'You will always receive payment confirmations', enabled: true, locked: true },
  ]);

  const toggleSetting = (
    settingsArray: ToggleSetting[],
    setSettingsArray: React.Dispatch<React.SetStateAction<ToggleSetting[]>>,
    id: string
  ) => {
    setSettingsArray(
      settingsArray.map((item) =>
        item.id === id && !item.locked ? { ...item, enabled: !item.enabled } : item
      )
    );
  };

  const ToggleSwitch = ({ enabled, locked }: { enabled: boolean; locked?: boolean }) => (
    <button
      disabled={locked}
      className={`relative w-12 h-7 rounded-full transition-colors duration-200 ${
        enabled ? 'bg-[#6FF0C4]' : 'bg-[#C6CFD9]/30'
      } ${locked ? 'opacity-50' : ''}`}
    >
      <div
        className={`absolute top-1 w-5 h-5 bg-white rounded-full transition-transform duration-200 ${
          enabled ? 'translate-x-6' : 'translate-x-1'
        }`}
      />
    </button>
  );

  const SettingsSection = ({
    title,
    items,
    onToggle,
  }: {
    title: string;
    items: ToggleSetting[];
    onToggle: (id: string) => void;
  }) => (
    <div className="mb-8">
      <h3
        className="text-[#C6CFD9] mb-3 px-1"
        style={{ fontSize: '0.8125rem', fontWeight: 600, letterSpacing: '0.05em' }}
      >
        {title.toUpperCase()}
      </h3>
      <div className="space-y-4">
        {items.map((item) => (
          <div
            key={item.id}
            onClick={() => !item.locked && onToggle(item.id)}
            className="bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl p-5 border border-white/5 flex items-start justify-between gap-4 transition-all duration-200 active:bg-[#050B12]"
          >
            <div className="flex-1">
              <p className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-1" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                {item.label}
              </p>
              <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                {item.description}
              </p>
            </div>
            <ToggleSwitch enabled={item.enabled} locked={item.locked} />
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-6 flex items-center gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Notifications
        </h1>
      </div>

      {/* Scrollable Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-8">
        <SettingsSection
          title="General"
          items={settings}
          onToggle={(id) => toggleSetting(settings, setSettings, id)}
        />

        <SettingsSection
          title="Service Updates"
          items={serviceUpdates}
          onToggle={(id) => toggleSetting(serviceUpdates, setServiceUpdates, id)}
        />

        <SettingsSection
          title="Reminders"
          items={reminders}
          onToggle={(id) => toggleSetting(reminders, setReminders, id)}
        />

        <SettingsSection
          title="Promotions"
          items={promotional}
          onToggle={(id) => toggleSetting(promotional, setPromotional, id)}
        />

        <SettingsSection
          title="System"
          items={system}
          onToggle={(id) => toggleSetting(system, setSystem, id)}
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


=== FILE: src/components/OnboardingFlow.tsx ===

import { useState } from 'react';
import { Zap, Shield, Sparkles, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-react';

interface OnboardingFlowProps {
  onComplete: () => void;
}

const screens = [
  {
    icon: Zap,
    title: 'Book Premium Detailing in Seconds',
    subtitle: 'Deep-clean car care brought to your driveway.',
  },
  {
    icon: Shield,
    title: 'Professional Detailers You Can Trust',
    subtitle: 'Certified professionals, premium results.',
  },
  {
    icon: Sparkles,
    title: 'Luxury Finish, Every Time',
    subtitle: 'Showroom shine delivered to your location.',
  },
];

export function OnboardingFlow({ onComplete }: OnboardingFlowProps) {
  const [currentScreen, setCurrentScreen] = useState(0);

  const handleNext = () => {
    if (currentScreen < screens.length - 1) {
      setCurrentScreen(currentScreen + 1);
    } else {
      onComplete();
    }
  };

  const screen = screens[currentScreen];
  const Icon = screen.icon;

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col items-center justify-center px-8 pb-32">
        {/* Icon */}
        <div className="mb-12 relative animate-fade-in-up">
          <Icon 
            className="w-24 h-24 text-[#6FF0C4]" 
            strokeWidth={1.2}
          />
          <div className="absolute inset-0 blur-2xl opacity-20 bg-[#6FF0C4]" />
        </div>

        {/* Title */}
        <h2 
          className="text-[#F5F7FA] text-center mb-5 px-4 animate-fade-in-up max-w-md tracking-wide"
          style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600, animationDelay: '100ms', opacity: 0 }}
        >
          {screen.title}
        </h2>

        {/* Subtitle */}
        <p 
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] text-center max-w-sm animate-fade-in-up"
          style={{ fontSize: '1rem', animationDelay: '200ms', opacity: 0 }}
        >
          {screen.subtitle}
        </p>
      </div>

      {/* Progress Dots */}
      <div className="flex justify-center gap-2.5 mb-10">
        {screens.map((_, index) => (
          <div
            key={index}
            className={`h-2 rounded-full transition-all duration-300 ${
              index === currentScreen 
                ? 'w-8 bg-[#6FF0C4]' 
                : 'w-2 bg-[#C6CFD9] opacity-30'
            }`}
          />
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* CTA Button */}
      <div className="px-6 pb-12">
        <button
          onClick={handleNext}
          className="w-full bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20 flex items-center justify-center gap-2"
          style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600, minHeight: '56px' }}
        >
          {currentScreen < screens.length - 1 ? 'Next' : 'Get Started'}
          <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5" strokeWidth={2.5} />
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, Car } from 'lucide-react';

interface OrdersHistoryScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
  onOrderDetails: (orderId: string) => void;
}

const orders = [
  {
    id: '1',
    service: 'Full Exterior Detail',
    car: '2022 BMW M4',
    license: 'ABC-123',
    date: 'Nov 16, 2:42 PM',
    price: '$213.57',
    status: 'completed',
  },
  {
    id: '2',
    service: 'Quick Wash',
    car: '2022 BMW M4',
    license: 'ABC-123',
    date: 'Nov 10, 11:30 AM',
    price: '$45.00',
    status: 'completed',
  },
  {
    id: '3',
    service: 'Interior Detail',
    car: '2021 Tesla Model 3',
    license: 'XYZ-789',
    date: 'Nov 3, 4:15 PM',
    price: '$120.00',
    status: 'completed',
  },
  {
    id: '4',
    service: 'Full Detail',
    car: '2023 Porsche 911',
    license: 'POR-911',
    date: 'Oct 28, 1:00 PM',
    price: '$285.00',
    status: 'completed',
  },
  {
    id: '5',
    service: 'Exterior Wash',
    car: '2022 BMW M4',
    license: 'ABC-123',
    date: 'Oct 15, 9:45 AM',
    price: '$65.00',
    status: 'canceled',
  },
];

export function OrdersHistoryScreen({ onBack, onOrderDetails }: OrdersHistoryScreenProps) {
  const getStatusColor = (status: string) => {
    switch (status) {
      case 'completed':
        return 'text-[#6FF0C4]';
      case 'scheduled':
        return 'text-[#1DA4F3]';
      case 'in-progress':
        return 'text-[#6FF0C4]';
      case 'canceled':
        return 'text-[#C6CFD9]';
      default:
        return 'text-[#C6CFD9]';
    }
  };

  const getStatusDot = (status: string) => {
    switch (status) {
      case 'completed':
        return 'bg-[#6FF0C4]';
      case 'scheduled':
        return 'bg-[#1DA4F3]';
      case 'in-progress':
        return 'bg-[#6FF0C4] animate-pulse';
      case 'canceled':
        return 'bg-[#C6CFD9]';
      default:
        return 'bg-[#C6CFD9]';
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-6 flex items-center gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors active:scale-95"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Your Bookings
        </h1>
      </div>

      {/* Scrollable Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-8">
        {orders.length > 0 ? (
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {orders.map((order) => (
              <button
                key={order.id}
                onClick={() => onOrderDetails(order.id)}
                className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl p-6 border border-white/5 transition-all duration-200 active:bg-[#050B12] hover:border-white/10"
              >
                <div className="flex items-start gap-4">
                  {/* Car Icon */}
                  <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-[#1DA4F3]/10 flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0">
                    <Car className="w-6 h-6 text-[#1DA4F3]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                  </div>

                  {/* Order Info */}
                  <div className="flex-1 text-left">
                    <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-2">
                      <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
                        {order.service}
                      </h3>
                      <span className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
                        {order.price}
                      </span>
                    </div>

                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9] mb-2" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                      {order.car} • {order.license}
                    </p>

                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                      <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                        {order.date}
                      </p>

                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <div className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${getStatusDot(order.status)}`} />
                        <span
                          className={`capitalize ${getStatusColor(order.status)}`}
                          style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', fontWeight: 500 }}
                        >
                          {order.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Chevron */}
                  <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9] flex-shrink-0 mt-1" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                </div>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        ) : (
          /* Empty State */
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-20">
            <Car className="w-16 h-16 text-[#C6CFD9] mb-4" strokeWidth={1} />
            <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-2" style={{ fontSize: '1.25rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
              No Bookings Yet
            </h3>
            <p className="text-[#C6CFD9] text-center" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>
              Your past detailing sessions will appear here.
            </p>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronLeft, Plus, Check } from 'lucide-react';
import { FaApple, FaCcVisa, FaCcMastercard } from 'react-icons/fa';

interface PaymentMethodScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
  onContinue: () => void;
  onAddCard: () => void;
  showPriceSummary?: boolean;
}

const savedCards = [
  { id: '1', type: 'visa', last4: '2741', expiry: '10/27' },
  { id: '2', type: 'mastercard', last4: '8392', expiry: '03/26' },
];

export function PaymentMethodScreen({ onBack, onContinue, onAddCard, showPriceSummary = true }: PaymentMethodScreenProps) {
  const [selectedCard, setSelectedCard] = useState<string>('apple-pay');

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-6 flex items-center gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Payment Method
        </h1>
      </div>

      {/* Scrollable Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-32">
        {/* Security Statement */}
        <p className="text-[#C6CFD9] text-center mb-6" style={{ fontSize: '0.8125rem' }}>
          Your payment information is encrypted and securely stored.
        </p>

        {/* Apple Pay */}
        <button
          onClick={() => setSelectedCard('apple-pay')}
          className={`w-full bg-black border py-4 rounded-full mb-6 transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] flex items-center justify-center gap-3 ${
            selectedCard === 'apple-pay'
              ? 'border-[#6FF0C4] shadow-lg shadow-[#6FF0C4]/20'
              : 'border-white/10'
          }`}
        >
          <FaApple className="w-6 h-6 text-white" />
          <span className="text-white" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
            Apple Pay
          </span>
        </button>

        {/* Divider */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mb-6">
          <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-[#C6CFD9]/20" />
          <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>OR</span>
          <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-[#C6CFD9]/20" />
        </div>

        {/* Saved Cards */}
        <div className="space-y-3 mb-4">
          {savedCards.map((card) => {
            const isSelected = selectedCard === card.id;
            const Icon = card.type === 'visa' ? FaCcVisa : FaCcMastercard;

            return (
              <button
                key={card.id}
                onClick={() => setSelectedCard(card.id)}
                className={`w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl p-5 transition-all duration-200 relative ${
                  isSelected
                    ? 'border-2 border-[#6FF0C4] shadow-lg shadow-[#6FF0C4]/20'
                    : 'border border-white/5 active:scale-[0.98]'
                }`}
              >
                {isSelected && (
                  <div className="absolute top-4 right-4 w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-[#6FF0C4] flex items-center justify-center">
                    <Check className="w-3 h-3 text-[#050B12]" strokeWidth={3} />
                  </div>
                )}

                <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                  <Icon className="w-12 h-12 text-white opacity-90" />
                  <div className="text-left flex-1">
                    <p className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-1" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                      {card.type === 'visa' ? 'Visa' : 'Mastercard'} •••• {card.last4}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                      Exp {card.expiry}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Add New Card */}
        <button
          onClick={onAddCard}
          className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl p-5 border border-dashed border-[#6FF0C4]/30 transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] hover:border-[#6FF0C4]/50"
        >
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-3">

              <Plus className="w-5 h-5 text-[#6FF0C4]" strokeWidth={2} />
            </div>
            <span className="text-[#6FF0C4]" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Add New Card
            </span>
          </div>
        </button>

        {/* Price Summary */}
        {showPriceSummary && (
          <div className="mt-8 bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl p-5 border border-white/5">
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <div className="flex justify-between">
                <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>Service</span>

                <span className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>$35.00</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex justify-between">
                <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>HST</span>
                <span className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>$24.57</span>
              </div>
              <div className="h-px bg-[#C6CFD9]/20 my-3" />
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                <span className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
                  Total
                </span>
                <span className="text-[#6FF0C4]" style={{ fontSize: '1.5rem', fontWeight: 700 }}>
                  $208.57
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Bottom CTA */}
      <div className="px-6 pb-8 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#050B12] via-[#050B12] to-transparent pt-6">
        <button
          onClick={onContinue}
          className="w-full bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20"
          style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600 }}
        >
          {showPriceSummary ? 'Complete Payment' : 'Save'}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

import { ChevronRight, User, Package, CreditCard, Bell, HelpCircle, Settings, LogOut, FileText, Shield, Car, ChevronLeft } from 'lucide-react';

interface ProfileScreenProps {
  onEditProfile: () => void;
  onOrders: () => void;
  onManageCars?: () => void;
  onPayment: () => void;
  onNotifications: () => void;
  onSupport: () => void;
  onSettings: () => void;
  onLogout: () => void;
  onBack?: () => void;
}

const menuSections = [
  {
    title: 'Account',
    items: [
      { icon: User, label: 'Personal Info', action: 'edit-profile' },
      { icon: Car, label: 'Manage Cars', action: 'manage-cars' },
      { icon: CreditCard, label: 'Payment Methods', action: 'payment' },
    ],
  },
  {
    title: 'Preferences',
    items: [
      { icon: Bell, label: 'Notifications', action: 'notifications' },
      { icon: Settings, label: 'Settings', action: 'settings' },
    ],
  },
  {
    title: 'Support',
    items: [
      { icon: HelpCircle, label: 'Help Center', action: 'support' },
      { icon: FileText, label: 'Terms of Service', action: 'terms' },
      { icon: Shield, label: 'Privacy Policy', action: 'privacy' },
    ],
  },
];

export function ProfileScreen({
  onEditProfile,
  onOrders,
  onManageCars,
  onPayment,
  onNotifications,
  onSupport,
  onSettings,
  onLogout,
  onBack,
}: ProfileScreenProps) {
  const handleAction = (action: string) => {
    switch (action) {
      case 'edit-profile':
        onEditProfile();
        break;
      case 'manage-cars':
        onManageCars?.();
        break;
      case 'payment':
        onPayment();
        break;
      case 'notifications':
        onNotifications();
        break;
      case 'settings':
        onSettings();
        break;
      case 'support':
        onSupport();
        break;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header with Back Button */}
      {onBack && (
        <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-4 flex items-center gap-4">
          <button
            onClick={onBack}
            className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors active:scale-95"
          >
            <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
          </button>
          <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
            Profile
          </h1>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Header with Profile */}
      <div className={onBack ? "px-6 pb-8" : "px-6 pt-16 pb-8"}>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
          {/* Profile Photo */}
          <div className="w-20 h-20 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-[#1DA4F3]/20 to-[#6FF0C4]/20 flex items-center justify-center ring-2 ring-[#6FF0C4]/40">
            <User className="w-10 h-10 text-[#6FF0C4]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
          </div>

          {/* User Info */}
          <div className="flex-1">
            <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-1.5" style={{ fontSize: '1.5rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
              Peeyush Yerremsetty
            </h1>
            <p className="text-[#C6CFD9] mb-1" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>
              meherpeeyush@gmail.com
            </p>
            <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>
              437-989-6480
            </p>
          </div>

          {/* Edit Button */}
          <button
            onClick={onEditProfile}
            className="text-[#6FF0C4] hover:text-[#6FF0C4]/80 transition-colors active:scale-95"
          >
            <Settings className="w-5 h-5" strokeWidth={1.5} />
          </button>

          >
            <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-[#1DA4F3]/10 flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0">
              <Package className="w-6 h-6 text-[#1DA4F3]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
            </div>
            <div className="flex-1 text-left">
              <p className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-1" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
                Your Orders
              </p>
              <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                View booking history & receipts
              </p>
            </div>
            <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9] flex-shrink-0" strokeWidth={1.5} />
          </button>
        </div>

        {menuSections.map((section, sectionIndex) => (
          <div key={sectionIndex} className="mb-8">
            {/* Section Title */}
            <h3
              className="text-[#C6CFD9] mb-4 px-1"
              style={{ fontSize: '0.8125rem', fontWeight: 600, letterSpacing: '0.05em' }}
            >
              {section.title.toUpperCase()}
            </h3>

            {/* Menu Items */}
            <div className="bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl border border-white/5 overflow-hidden">
              {section.items.map((item, itemIndex) => {
                const Icon = item.icon;
                const isLast = itemIndex === section.items.length - 1;

                return (
                  <button
                    key={itemIndex}
                    onClick={() => handleAction(item.action)}
                    className={`w-full flex items-center gap-4 px-6 py-4.5 transition-all duration-200 active:bg-[#050B12] hover:bg-[#0A1A2F]/80 ${
                      !isLast ? 'border-b border-[#C6CFD9]/10' : ''

                    <Icon className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9] flex-shrink-0" strokeWidth={1.5} />

                      {item.label}
                    </span>
                    <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9] flex-shrink-0" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}

        {/* Logout Button */}
        <button
          onClick={onLogout}
          className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl border border-white/5 px-6 py-4 flex items-center justify-center gap-3 transition-all duration-200 active:bg-[#050B12] hover:border-red-500/30"
          style={{ minHeight: '56px' }}
        >
          <LogOut className="w-5 h-5 text-[#C6CFD9]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
          <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
            Log Out
          </span>
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronLeft, Car, Plus, Check } from 'lucide-react';

interface SelectCarScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
  onAddCar: () => void;
  onContinue: () => void;
}

const savedCars = [
  {
    id: '1',
    model: '2022 BMW M4',
    details: 'Competition Package',
    license: 'ABC-123',
    color: 'Black Sapphire Metallic',
  },
  {
    id: '2',
    model: '2021 Tesla Model 3',
    details: 'Performance',
    license: 'XYZ-789',
    color: 'Pearl White Multi-Coat',
  },
  {
    id: '3',
    model: '2023 Porsche 911',
    details: 'Carrera S',
    license: 'POR-911',
    color: 'GT Silver Metallic',
  },
];

export function SelectCarScreen({ onBack, onAddCar, onContinue }: SelectCarScreenProps) {
  const [selectedCar, setSelectedCar] = useState<string>('1');

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">

          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors active:scale-95"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Select Your Car
        </h1>
      </div>

        {/* Vehicle Cards */}
        <div className="space-y-4 mb-6">

            return (
              <button
                key={car.id}
                onClick={() => setSelectedCar(car.id)}
                className={`w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-3xl p-6 transition-all duration-200 relative ${
                  isSelected
                    ? 'border-2 border-[#6FF0C4] shadow-lg shadow-[#6FF0C4]/20'

                }`}

                  <div className="absolute top-6 right-6 w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-[#6FF0C4] flex items-center justify-center">
                    <Check className="w-4 h-4 text-[#050B12]" strokeWidth={3} />
                  </div>
                )}

                {/* Car Icon */}
                <div className="mb-6 relative inline-block">
                  <Car 
                    className={`w-14 h-14 ${isSelected ? 'text-[#6FF0C4]' : 'text-[#1DA4F3]'}`}
                    strokeWidth={1}
                  />
                  {isSelected && (
                    <div className="absolute inset-0 blur-2xl opacity-20 bg-[#6FF0C4]" />
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Car Info */}
                <div className="text-left">
                  <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-3" style={{ fontSize: '1.25rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
                    {car.model}
                  </h3>
                  <div className="space-y-1.5">
                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                      {car.details}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                      License: {car.license}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>
                      {car.color}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Add Car Card */}
        <button
          onClick={onAddCar}
          className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-3xl p-6 border border-dashed border-[#6FF0C4]/30 transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] hover:border-[#6FF0C4]/50 hover:bg-[#0A1A2F]/80"
        >
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-4 py-4">
            <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-[#6FF0C4]/10 flex items-center justify-center">
              <Plus className="w-8 h-8 text-[#6FF0C4]" strokeWidth={1.5} />
            </div>
            <p className="text-[#6FF0C4]" style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
              Add a Car
            </p>
          </div>
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Bottom CTA */}
      <div className="px-6 pb-8 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#050B12] via-[#050B12] to-transparent pt-6">
        <button
          onClick={onContinue}
          className="w-full bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20"
          style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600, minHeight: '56px' }}
        >
          Continue
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronLeft, Droplet, Sparkles, Star, Award, Check } from 'lucide-react';

interface ServiceSelectionScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
  onContinue: () => void;
}

const services = [
  {
    id: 'quick-wash',
    title: 'Quick Wash',
    price: '$29',
    description: 'Fast exterior clean.',
    icon: Droplet,
  },
  {
    id: 'exterior-wash',
    title: 'Exterior Wash',
    price: '$49',
    description: 'Complete exterior detail and polish.',
    icon: Star,
  },
  {
    id: 'full-detail',
    title: 'Full Detail',
    price: '$79',
    description: 'Deep clean inside and out.',
    icon: Sparkles,
  },
  {
    id: 'luxury-package',
    title: 'Luxury Package',
    price: '$149',
    description: 'Premium showroom shine.',
    icon: Award,
  },
];

const addOns = [
  { id: 'tire-shine', label: 'Tire Shine', price: '+$10' },
  { id: 'wax-finish', label: 'Wax Finish', price: '+$20' },
  { id: 'clay-bar', label: 'Clay Bar Treatment', price: '+$35' },
  { id: 'pet-hair', label: 'Pet Hair Removal', price: '+$15' },
];

export function ServiceSelectionScreen({ onBack, onContinue }: ServiceSelectionScreenProps) {
  const [selectedService, setSelectedService] = useState<string>('');
  const [selectedAddOns, setSelectedAddOns] = useState<string[]>([]);

  const toggleAddOn = (id: string) => {
    setSelectedAddOns(prev =>
      prev.includes(id) ? prev.filter(item => item !== id) : [...prev, id]
    );
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="px-6 pt-16 pb-6 flex items-center gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors active:scale-95"
        >
          <ChevronLeft className="w-6 h-6" strokeWidth={1.5} />
        </button>
        <h1 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.75rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
          Select a Service
        </h1>
      </div>

      {/* Scrollable Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-32">
        {/* Service Cards */}
        <div className="space-y-4 mb-8">
          {services.map((service) => {
            const Icon = service.icon;
            const isSelected = selectedService === service.id;

            return (
              <button
                key={service.id}
                onClick={() => setSelectedService(service.id)}
                className={`w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-3xl p-6 transition-all duration-200 relative ${
                  isSelected
                    ? 'border-2 border-[#6FF0C4] shadow-lg shadow-[#6FF0C4]/20'
                    : 'border border-white/5 active:scale-[0.98] hover:border-white/10'
                }`}
                style={{ minHeight: '120px' }}
              >
                {/* Selection Checkmark */}
                {isSelected && (
                  <div className="absolute top-5 right-5 w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-[#6FF0C4] flex items-center justify-center">
                    <Check className="w-4 h-4 text-[#050B12]" strokeWidth={3} />
                  </div>
                )}

                <div className="flex items-start gap-5">
                  {/* Icon */}
                  <div className="flex-shrink-0">
                    <div className="relative">
                      <Icon 
                        className={`w-12 h-12 ${isSelected ? 'text-[#6FF0C4]' : 'text-[#1DA4F3]'}`}
                        strokeWidth={1.2}
                      />
                      {isSelected && (
                        <div className="absolute inset-0 blur-xl opacity-30 bg-[#6FF0C4]" />
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Content */}
                  <div className="flex-1 text-left">
                    <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-2">
                      <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1.25rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
                        {service.title}
                      </h3>
                    </div>
                    <p 
                      className={`mb-2.5 ${isSelected ? 'text-[#6FF0C4]' : 'text-[#1DA4F3]'}`}
                      style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 600 }}
                    >
                      {service.price}+
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>
                      {service.description}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Add-Ons Section */}
        <div className="mb-8">
          <h3 className="text-[#F5F7FA] mb-5" style={{ fontSize: '1.125rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>
            Add-Ons
          </h3>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {addOns.map((addOn) => {
              const isSelected = selectedAddOns.includes(addOn.id);

              return (
                <button
                  key={addOn.id}
                  onClick={() => toggleAddOn(addOn.id)}
                  className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] rounded-2xl p-5 border border-white/5 flex items-center justify-between transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] hover:border-white/10"
                  style={{ minHeight: '64px' }}
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div
                      className={`w-6 h-6 rounded-full border-2 transition-all duration-200 flex items-center justify-center ${
                        isSelected
                          ? 'bg-[#6FF0C4] border-[#6FF0C4]'
                          : 'border-[#C6CFD9]/30'
                      }`}
                    >
                      {isSelected && (
                        <Check className="w-4 h-4 text-[#050B12]" strokeWidth={3} />
                      )}
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-[#F5F7FA]" style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                      {addOn.label}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.9375rem' }}>
                    {addOn.price}
                  </span>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Bottom CTA */}
      <div className="px-6 pb-8 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#050B12] via-[#050B12] to-transparent pt-6">
        <button
          onClick={onContinue}
          disabled={!selectedService}
          className={`w-full py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 ${
            selectedService
              ? 'bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20'
              : 'bg-[#0A1A2F] text-[#C6CFD9]/50 cursor-not-allowed'
          }`}
          style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600, minHeight: '56px' }}
        >
          Continue
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { Eye, EyeOff } from 'lucide-react';
import { FaApple, FaGoogle } from 'react-icons/fa';

interface SignInScreenProps {
  onSignIn: () => void;
}

export function SignInScreen({ onSignIn }: SignInScreenProps) {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    onSignIn();
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0A1A2F] to-[#050B12] overflow-auto">
      <div className="min-h-full flex flex-col px-6 py-12">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="mb-12 pt-8">
          <h1 
            className="text-[#F5F7FA] tracking-wide"
            style={{ fontSize: '2rem', fontWeight: 700 }}
          >
            Sign In
          </h1>
        </div>

        {/* Form */}
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
          <div className="space-y-5">
            {/* Email Field */}
            <div>
              <input
                type="email"
                placeholder="Email"
                value={email}
                onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9] focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all"
                style={{ fontSize: '1rem', minHeight: '56px' }}
              />
            </div>

            {/* Password Field */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
                placeholder="Password"
                value={password}
                onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full bg-[#0A1A2F] border border-[#C6CFD9]/20 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 text-[#F5F7FA] placeholder:text-[#C6CFD9] focus:border-[#1DA4F3] focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#1DA4F3]/50 transition-all pr-14"
                style={{ fontSize: '1rem', minHeight: '56px' }}
              />
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                className="absolute right-5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors active:scale-95"
              >
                {showPassword ? (
                  <EyeOff className="w-5 h-5" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                ) : (
                  <Eye className="w-5 h-5" strokeWidth={1.5} />
                )}
              </button>
            </div>

            {/* Forgot Password */}
            <div className="flex justify-end">
              <button
                type="button"
                className="text-[#C6CFD9] hover:text-[#6FF0C4] transition-colors active:scale-95"
                style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}
              >
                Forgot Password?
              </button>
            </div>

            {/* Sign In Button */}
            <button
              type="submit"
              className="w-full bg-[#1DA4F3] text-white py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] shadow-lg shadow-[#1DA4F3]/20 mt-2"
              style={{ fontSize: '1.0625rem', fontWeight: 600, minHeight: '56px' }}
            >
              Sign In
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* Divider */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4 my-10">
            <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-[#C6CFD9]/20" />
            <span className="text-[#C6CFD9]" style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem' }}>OR</span>
            <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-[#C6CFD9]/20" />
          </div>

          {/* Social Sign In */}
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {/* Apple Sign In */}
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={onSignIn}
              className="w-full bg-black border border-white/10 text-white py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] flex items-center justify-center gap-3"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500, minHeight: '56px' }}
            >

              Continue with Apple
            </button>

              onClick={onSignIn}
              className="w-full bg-white text-black py-4 rounded-full transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] flex items-center justify-center gap-3 border border-[#C6CFD9]/20"
              style={{ fontSize: '1rem', fontWeight: 500, minHeight: '56px' }}
